https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/b9297af2-c1a5-4637-9e74-0ad895a3d984
Excessive re-renders on pointer move during line editing
There are two things that cause unnecessary re-renders while moving the pointer while in the line editor:
- A new `editingLinearElement` is returned each time [here](https://github.com/excalidraw/excalidraw/blob/678dff25eddfc43319299495556ab9f6029bc719/packages/element/src/linearElementEditor.ts#L1043-L1047) even if nothing's changed. The new reference of `editingLinearElement` is then checked against the one in appState [here](https://github.com/excalidraw/excalidraw/blob/678dff25eddfc43319299495556ab9f6029bc719/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx#L5860-L5863).
- Always executing `setState` [here](https://github.com/excalidraw/excalidraw/blob/678dff25eddfc43319299495556ab9f6029bc719/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx#L5878-L5883) even if nothing's changed.
Bug: "suggested bindings box" shows in line editor (not arrow) while pressing alt to add a point
The type of the element is not checked [here](https://github.com/excalidraw/excalidraw/blob/678dff25eddfc43319299495556ab9f6029bc719/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx#L5873-L5877)

    90	/**
    91	 * Normalizes line points so that the start point is at [0,0]. This is
    92	 * expected in various parts of the codebase.
    93	 *
    94	 * Also returns the offsets - [0,0] if no normalization needed.
    95	 *
    96	 * @private
    97	 */
    98	const getNormalizedPoints = ({
    99	  points,
   100	}: {
   101	  points: ExcalidrawLinearElement["points"];
   102	}): {
   103	  points: LocalPoint[];
   104	  offsetX: number;
   105	  offsetY: number;
   106	} => {
   107	  const offsetX = points[0][0];
   108	  const offsetY = points[0][1];
   109	
   110	  return {
   111	    points: points.map((p) => {
   112	      return pointFrom(p[0] - offsetX, p[1] - offsetY);
   113	    }),
   114	    offsetX,
   115	    offsetY,
   116	  };
   117	};

   119	export class LinearElementEditor {

   153	  constructor(
   154	    element: NonDeleted<ExcalidrawLinearElement>,
   155	    elementsMap: ElementsMap,
   156	  ) {
   157	    this.elementId = element.id as string & {
   158	      _brand: "excalidrawLinearElementId";
   159	    };
   160	    if (!pointsEqual(element.points[0], pointFrom(0, 0))) {
   161	      console.error("Linear element is not normalized", Error().stack);
   162	      mutateElement(
   163	        element,
   164	        elementsMap,
   165	        LinearElementEditor.getNormalizeElementPointsAndCoords(element),
   166	      );
   167	    }
   168	    this.selectedPointsIndices = null;
   169	    this.lastUncommittedPoint = null;
   170	    this.isDragging = false;
   171	    this.pointerOffset = { x: 0, y: 0 };
   172	    this.startBindingElement = "keep";
   173	    this.endBindingElement = "keep";

   186	    this.hoverPointIndex = -1;
   187	    this.segmentMidPointHoveredCoords = null;
   188	    this.elbowed = isElbowArrow(element) && element.elbowed;
   189	    this.customLineAngle = null;

   201	  static getElement<T extends ExcalidrawLinearElement>(
   202	    id: InstanceType<typeof LinearElementEditor>["elementId"],
   203	    elementsMap: ElementsMap,
   204	  ): T | null {

   206	    if (element) {

   211	
   212	  static handleBoxSelection(
   213	    event: PointerEvent,
   214	    appState: AppState,
   215	    setState: React.Component<any, AppState>["setState"],
   216	    elementsMap: NonDeletedSceneElementsMap,
   217	  ) {
   218	    if (!appState.editingLinearElement || !appState.selectionElement) {
   219	      return false;
   220	    }
   221	    const { editingLinearElement } = appState;
   222	    const { selectedPointsIndices, elementId } = editingLinearElement;
   223	
   224	    const element = LinearElementEditor.getElement(elementId, elementsMap);
   225	    if (!element) {
   226	      return false;
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    const [selectionX1, selectionY1, selectionX2, selectionY2] =
   230	      getElementAbsoluteCoords(appState.selectionElement, elementsMap);
   231	
   232	    const pointsSceneCoords = LinearElementEditor.getPointsGlobalCoordinates(
   233	      element,
   234	      elementsMap,
   235	    );
   236	
   237	    const nextSelectedPoints = pointsSceneCoords
   238	      .reduce((acc: number[], point, index) => {
   239	        if (
   240	          (point[0] >= selectionX1 &&
   241	            point[0] <= selectionX2 &&
   242	            point[1] >= selectionY1 &&
   243	            point[1] <= selectionY2) ||
   244	          (event.shiftKey && selectedPointsIndices?.includes(index))
   245	        ) {
   246	          acc.push(index);
   247	        }
   248	
   249	        return acc;
   250	      }, [])
   251	      .filter((index) => {
   252	        if (
   253	          isElbowArrow(element) &&
   254	          index !== 0 &&
   255	          index !== element.points.length - 1
   256	        ) {
   257	          return false;
   258	        }
   259	        return true;
   260	      });
   261	
   262	    setState({
   263	      editingLinearElement: {
   264	        ...editingLinearElement,
   265	        selectedPointsIndices: nextSelectedPoints.length
   266	          ? nextSelectedPoints
   267	          : null,
   268	      },
   269	    });
   270	  }
   271	
   272	  /**
   273	   * @returns whether point was dragged
   274	   */
   275	  static handlePointDragging(
   276	    event: PointerEvent,
   277	    app: AppClassProperties,
   278	    scenePointerX: number,
   279	    scenePointerY: number,
   280	    linearElementEditor: LinearElementEditor,
   281	  ): Pick<AppState, keyof AppState> | null {
   282	    if (!linearElementEditor) {
   283	      return null;
   284	    }
   285	    const { elementId } = linearElementEditor;
   286	    const elementsMap = app.scene.getNonDeletedElementsMap();
   287	    const element = LinearElementEditor.getElement(elementId, elementsMap);
   288	    let customLineAngle = linearElementEditor.customLineAngle;
   289	    if (!element) {
   290	      return null;
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    if (
   294	      isElbowArrow(element) &&
   295	      !linearElementEditor.pointerDownState.lastClickedIsEndPoint &&
   296	      linearElementEditor.pointerDownState.lastClickedPoint !== 0
   297	    ) {
   298	      return null;
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    const selectedPointsIndices = isElbowArrow(element)
   302	      ? [
   303	          !!linearElementEditor.selectedPointsIndices?.includes(0)
   304	            ? 0
   305	            : undefined,
   306	          !!linearElementEditor.selectedPointsIndices?.find((idx) => idx > 0)
   307	            ? element.points.length - 1
   308	            : undefined,
   309	        ].filter((idx): idx is number => idx !== undefined)
   310	      : linearElementEditor.selectedPointsIndices;
   311	    const lastClickedPoint = isElbowArrow(element)
   312	      ? linearElementEditor.pointerDownState.lastClickedPoint > 0
   313	        ? element.points.length - 1
   314	        : 0
   315	      : linearElementEditor.pointerDownState.lastClickedPoint;
   316	
   317	    // point that's being dragged (out of all selected points)
   318	    const draggingPoint = element.points[lastClickedPoint];
   319	
   320	    if (selectedPointsIndices && draggingPoint) {
   321	      if (
   322	        shouldRotateWithDiscreteAngle(event) &&
   323	        selectedPointsIndices.length === 1 &&
   324	        element.points.length > 1
   325	      ) {
   326	        const selectedIndex = selectedPointsIndices[0];
   327	        const referencePoint =
   328	          element.points[selectedIndex === 0 ? 1 : selectedIndex - 1];
   329	        customLineAngle =
   330	          linearElementEditor.customLineAngle ??
   331	          Math.atan2(
   332	            element.points[selectedIndex][1] - referencePoint[1],
   333	            element.points[selectedIndex][0] - referencePoint[0],
   334	          );
   335	
   336	        const [width, height] = LinearElementEditor._getShiftLockedDelta(
   337	          element,
   338	          elementsMap,
   339	          referencePoint,
   340	          pointFrom(scenePointerX, scenePointerY),
   341	          event[KEYS.CTRL_OR_CMD] ? null : app.getEffectiveGridSize(),
   342	          customLineAngle,
   343	        );
   344	
   345	        LinearElementEditor.movePoints(
   346	          element,
   347	          app.scene,
   348	          new Map([
   349	            [
   350	              selectedIndex,
   351	              {
   352	                point: pointFrom(
   353	                  width + referencePoint[0],
   354	                  height + referencePoint[1],
   355	                ),
   356	                isDragging: selectedIndex === lastClickedPoint,
   357	              },
   358	            ],
   359	          ]),
   360	        );
   361	      } else {
   362	        const newDraggingPointPosition = LinearElementEditor.createPointAt(
   363	          element,
   364	          elementsMap,
   365	          scenePointerX - linearElementEditor.pointerOffset.x,
   366	          scenePointerY - linearElementEditor.pointerOffset.y,
   367	          event[KEYS.CTRL_OR_CMD] ? null : app.getEffectiveGridSize(),
   368	        );
   369	
   370	        const deltaX = newDraggingPointPosition[0] - draggingPoint[0];
   371	        const deltaY = newDraggingPointPosition[1] - draggingPoint[1];
   372	
   373	        LinearElementEditor.movePoints(
   374	          element,
   375	          app.scene,
   376	          new Map(
   377	            selectedPointsIndices.map((pointIndex) => {
   378	              const newPointPosition: LocalPoint =
   379	                pointIndex === lastClickedPoint
   380	                  ? LinearElementEditor.createPointAt(
   381	                      element,
   382	                      elementsMap,
   383	                      scenePointerX - linearElementEditor.pointerOffset.x,
   384	                      scenePointerY - linearElementEditor.pointerOffset.y,
   385	                      event[KEYS.CTRL_OR_CMD]
   386	                        ? null
   387	                        : app.getEffectiveGridSize(),
   388	                    )
   389	                  : pointFrom(
   390	                      element.points[pointIndex][0] + deltaX,
   391	                      element.points[pointIndex][1] + deltaY,
   392	                    );
   393	              return [
   394	                pointIndex,
   395	                {
   396	                  point: newPointPosition,
   397	                  isDragging: pointIndex === lastClickedPoint,
   398	                },
   399	              ];
   400	            }),
   401	          ),
   402	        );
   403	      }
   404	
   405	      const boundTextElement = getBoundTextElement(element, elementsMap);
   406	      if (boundTextElement) {
   407	        handleBindTextResize(element, app.scene, false);
   408	      }
   409	
   410	      // suggest bindings for first and last point if selected
   411	      let suggestedBindings: ExcalidrawBindableElement[] = [];
   412	      if (isBindingElement(element, false)) {
   413	        const firstSelectedIndex = selectedPointsIndices[0] === 0;
   414	        const lastSelectedIndex =
   415	          selectedPointsIndices[selectedPointsIndices.length - 1] ===
   416	          element.points.length - 1;
   417	        const coords: { x: number; y: number }[] = [];
   418	
   419	        if (!firstSelectedIndex !== !lastSelectedIndex) {
   420	          coords.push({ x: scenePointerX, y: scenePointerY });
   421	        } else {
   422	          if (firstSelectedIndex) {
   423	            coords.push(
   424	              tupleToCoors(
   425	                LinearElementEditor.getPointGlobalCoordinates(
   426	                  element,
   427	                  element.points[0],
   428	                  elementsMap,
   429	                ),
   430	              ),
   431	            );
   432	          }
   433	
   434	          if (lastSelectedIndex) {
   435	            coords.push(
   436	              tupleToCoors(
   437	                LinearElementEditor.getPointGlobalCoordinates(
   438	                  element,
   439	                  element.points[
   440	                    selectedPointsIndices[selectedPointsIndices.length - 1]
   441	                  ],
   442	                  elementsMap,
   443	                ),
   444	              ),
   445	            );
   446	          }
   447	        }
   448	
   449	        if (coords.length) {
   450	          suggestedBindings = maybeSuggestBindingsForLinearElementAtCoords(
   451	            element,
   452	            coords,
   453	            app.scene,
   454	            app.state.zoom,
   455	          );
   456	        }
   457	      }
   458	
   459	      const newLinearElementEditor = {
   460	        ...linearElementEditor,
   461	        selectedPointsIndices,
   462	        segmentMidPointHoveredCoords:
   463	          lastClickedPoint !== 0 &&
   464	          lastClickedPoint !== element.points.length - 1
   465	            ? this.getPointGlobalCoordinates(
   466	                element,
   467	                draggingPoint,
   468	                elementsMap,
   469	              )
   470	            : null,
   471	        hoverPointIndex:
   472	          lastClickedPoint === 0 ||
   473	          lastClickedPoint === element.points.length - 1
   474	            ? lastClickedPoint
   475	            : -1,
   476	        isDragging: true,
   477	        customLineAngle,
   478	      };
   479	
   480	      return {
   481	        ...app.state,
   482	        editingLinearElement: app.state.editingLinearElement
   483	          ? newLinearElementEditor
   484	          : null,
   485	        selectedLinearElement: newLinearElementEditor,
   486	        suggestedBindings,
   487	      };
   488	    }
   489	
   490	    return null;
   491	  }

Now I understand the issues. Let me analyze each problem mentioned in the PR description:

1. **Bug: deleting all points from within line editor throws**
   - The issue is that `handleHoverSelectedLinearElement` was used to handle pointer away, but now it doesn't fire when the pointer is away while line-editing.

2. **Excessive re-renders on pointer move during line editing**
   - Two issues: 
     - A new `editingLinearElement` is returned each time in `linearElementEditor.ts` even if nothing's changed
     - Always executing `setState` even if nothing's changed

3. **Bug: "suggested bindings box" shows in line editor (not arrow) while pressing alt to add a point**
   - The type of the element is not checked properly

Now I understand the issues. Let me write a summary and then implement the fixes:

## Summary of Issues

1. **Issue 1**: When deleting all points from the line editor, the hovered point remains visible because `handleHoverSelectedLinearElement` is not called when the pointer is away during line editing.

2. **Issue 2**: Excessive re-renders occur because:
   - The `handlePointerMove` method always returns a new `editingLinearElement` object even when nothing changes (lines 1043-1046 and 1094-1097)
   - The `setState` call in App.tsx (lines 5878-5882) always executes even if the `editingLinearElement` hasn't changed

3. **Issue 3**: The "suggested bindings box" appears for non-arrow line elements because the type of element is not properly checked before calling `maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor` (line 5885)

Let me now implement the fixes:

## Fix for Issue 1
The issue is that when we're in line editing mode, the `handleHoverSelectedLinearElement` is not called to reset the hover state when the pointer moves away. We need to add logic to handle the pointer away scenario.

Let me examine the current pointer move handling logic:

"""
Fix the three issues described in the PR:

1. Line editor point remains hovered when deleting all points
2. Excessive re-renders on pointer move during line editing
3. "suggested bindings box" shows in line editor (not arrow) while pressing alt to add a point
"""

import os

def fix_issue1():
    """Fix Issue 1: Line editor point remains hovered"""
    print("=== Fixing Issue 1: Line editor point remains hovered ===")
    
    # The issue is that handleHoverSelectedLinearElement is not called during line editing
    # to handle pointer away. We need to add a call to reset hover state when pointer is away.
    
    # Read App.tsx around the handleCursor method
    with open("/testbed/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx", "r") as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Find the handleCursor method and add logic to handle pointer away during line editing
    handle_cursor_start = content.find("private handleCursor")
    if handle_cursor_start == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find handleCursor method")
        return
    
    # Look for the section where pointer move is handled
    pointer_move_section_start = content.find("// Dragging logic executes at lower fps", handle_cursor_start)
    if pointer_move_section_start == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find pointer move section")
        return
    
    # Find where we should inject the fix - after the editingLinearElement handling
    editing_linear_section_end = content.find("}", pointer_move_section_start)
    
    # Create the fix
    fix_code = '"'"''"'"''"'"'
    // Fix for Issue 1: Reset hover state when pointer is away during line editing
    if (this.state.editingLinearElement && !hitElement) {
      // Reset hover point index when pointer is away from the element
      const newEditingLinearElement = {
        ...this.state.editingLinearElement,
        hoverPointIndex: -1,
        segmentMidPointHoveredCoords: null,
      };
      if (newEditingLinearElement !== this.state.editingLinearElement) {
        this.setState({
          editingLinearElement: newEditingLinearElement,
        });
      }
    }'"'"''"'"''"'"'
    
    # Insert the fix after the editingLinearElement section
    new_content = content[:editing_linear_section_end + 1] + fix_code + content[editing_linear_section_end + 1:]
    
    # Write the modified content back
    with open("/testbed/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx", "w") as f:
        f.write(new_content)
    
    print("✓ Added pointer away handling for line editor")

def fix_issue2():
    """Fix Issue 2: Excessive re-renders"""
    print("\n=== Fixing Issue 2: Excessive re-renders ===")
    
    # Fix 2.1: Return same object reference if nothing changed in handlePointerMove
    with open("/testbed/packages/element/src/linearElementEditor.ts", "r") as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Find the handlePointerMove method
    handle_pointer_move_start = content.find("static handlePointerMove(")
    if handle_pointer_move_start == -1:

    # Find the specific return statement that creates new reference
    problematic_return_start = content.find("return {\n        ...appState.editingLinearElement,\n        lastUncommittedPoint: null,\n      };", handle_pointer_move_start)
    
    if problematic_return_start == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find problematic return statement")
        return
    
    # Fix the return statement to avoid unnecessary re-renders
    fixed_return = '"'"''"'"''"'"'      const currentEditor = appState.editingLinearElement;
      // Only return new object if lastUncommittedPoint has changed
      if (currentEditor.lastUncommittedPoint === null) {
        return currentEditor;
      }
      return {
        ...currentEditor,
        lastUncommittedPoint: null,
      };'"'"''"'"''"'"'
    
    # Find the exact lines to replace
    lines = content[problematic_return_start:].split('"'"'\n'"'"', 10)
    old_code = '"'"'\n'"'"'.join(lines[:4])
    
    new_content = content.replace(old_code, fixed_return, 1)
    
    # Fix 2.2: Add proper equality check in App.tsx
    with open("/testbed/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx", "r") as f:
        app_content = f.read()

    equality_check_start = app_content.find("editingLinearElement !== this.state.editingLinearElement")
    if equality_check_start == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find equality check")

    # Replace with a deep equality check or property comparison
    # For simplicity, let'"'"'s check if meaningful properties changed
    fixed_check = '"'"''"'"''"'"'editingLinearElement && 
        (editingLinearElement.lastUncommittedPoint !== this.state.editingLinearElement?.lastUncommittedPoint ||
         editingLinearElement.hoverPointIndex !== this.state.editingLinearElement?.hoverPointIndex ||
         editingLinearElement.segmentMidPointHoveredCoords !== this.state.editingLinearElement?.segmentMidPointHoveredCoords)'"'"''"'"''"'"'
    
    # Find the exact context
    context_start = app_content.rfind("if (", 0, equality_check_start)
    context_end = app_content.find(") {", equality_check_start) + 2
    old_if_statement = app_content[context_start:context_end]

def fix_issue3():
    """Fix Issue 3: Suggested bindings for non-arrows"""
    print("\n=== Fixing Issue 3: Suggested bindings for non-arrows ===")
    
    with open("/testbed/packages/excalidraw/components/App.tsx", "r") as f:
        content = f.read()
    
    # Find the maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor call during line editing
    cursor_call_start = content.find("if (editingLinearElement?.lastUncommittedPoint != null) {")
    if cursor_call_start == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor call")
        return
    
    # Find the elementId to get the element
    editing_section_start = content.rfind("const editingLinearElement = LinearElementEditor.handlePointerMove", 0, cursor_call_start)
    element_line = content.find("const element = LinearElementEditor.getElement", editing_section_start, cursor_call_start)
    
    if element_line == -1:
        print("ERROR: Could not find element retrieval")
        return
    
    # We need to modify the maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor call to check if the element is a binding element
    old_code_block = '"'"''"'"''"'"'      if (editingLinearElement?.lastUncommittedPoint != null) {
        this.maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor(
          scenePointer,
          editingLinearElement.elbowed,
        );
      }'"'"''"'"''"'"'
    
    fixed_code_block = '"'"''"'"''"'"'      if (editingLinearElement?.lastUncommittedPoint != null) {
        // Fix for Issue 3: Only suggest bindings for binding elements (arrows)
        const element = LinearElementEditor.getElement(editingLinearElement.elementId, this.scene.getNonDeletedElementsMap());
        if (element && isBindingElement(element, false)) {
          this.maybeSuggestBindingAtCursor(
            scenePointer,
            editingLinearElement.elbowed,

    print("\n=== Checking Code Compilation ===")
